d[c[0]]=c[1]
}return d

var changeStyle=function(c,b){var a=c.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.children;
c.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.onmouseout=resetStyle;
applyStyle(a,b)
};
var resetStyle=function(b){var a=b.currentTarget.firstElementChild.children;
applyStyle(a,"reset")
};
var applyStyle=function(a,c){for(var b=0;
b<a.length;
b++){if(a[b].classList.value.indexOf("feature-content__heading")>-1||a[b].classList.value.indexOf("related-content__item-heading")>-1){if(c=="in"){a[b].classList.remove("feature-content__border-bottom--show");
a[b].classList.add("feature-content__border-bottom--hide")
}else{if(c=="out"){a[b].classList.remove("feature-content__border-bottom--hide");
a[b].classList.add("feature-content__border-bottom--show")
}else{if(c=="reset"){a[b].classList.remove("feature-content__border-bottom--hide");
a[b].classList.remove("feature-content__border-bottom--show")
}}}}}};
function isValidPath(a){return a.indexOf(".html")>-1&&(!a.startsWith("http"))&&(!a.startsWith("www"))
}if(!String.prototype.startsWith){String.prototype.startsWith=function(b,a){a=a||0;
return this.indexOf(b,a)===a
}

$(this).parent().removeClass("active")
});
$(document).on("mouseup",function(){$(".marketingconsent-tooltip").removeClass("active")
})
});
